                adUnits.push({
                network: dfpNetwork,
                adunit: 'PokemonGo_Mobile_300x250_Extra_3',
                size: [[300, 250]],
                code: 'div-ad-PokemonGo_Mobile_300x250_Extra_3',
                assignToVariableName: false // false if not in use
            }); 
                adUnits.push({
                network: dfpNetwork,
                adunit: 'PokemonGo_Mobile_300x250_Extra_4',
                size: [[300, 250]],
                code: 'div-ad-PokemonGo_Mobile_300x250_Extra_4',
                assignToVariableName: false // false if not in use
            }); 
               adUnits.push({
                network: dfpNetwork,
                adunit: 'PokemonGo_Mobile_320x50_Top',
                size: [[320, 50]],
                code: 'div-ad-PokemonGo_Mobile_320x50_Top',
                assignToVariableName: false // false if not in use
            }); 
                adUnits.push({
                network: dfpNetwork,
                adunit: 'PokemonGo_Mobile_320x50_Floating',
                size: [[320, 50]],
                code: 'div-ad-PokemonGo_Mobile_320x50_Floating',
                assignToVariableName: false // false if not in use
            }); 
        
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                            adUnits.push({
                network: dfpNetwork,
                adunit: 'PokemonGo_Mobile_300x250_BTF_1',
                size: [[300, 250]],
                code: 'div-ad-PokemonGo_Mobile_300x250_BTF_1',
                assignToVariableName: false // false if not in use
            });  
                                                                                              adUnits.push({
                network: dfpNetwork,
                adunit: 'PokemonGo_Mobile_300x250_BTF_2',
                size: [[300, 250]],
                code: 'div-ad-PokemonGo_Mobile_300x250_BTF_2',
                assignToVariableName: false // false if not in use
            }); 
                                                                                              adUnits.push({
                network: dfpNetwork,
                adunit: 'PokemonGo_Mobile_300x250_Extra_1',
                size: [[300, 250]],
                code: 'div-ad-PokemonGo_Mobile_300x250_Extra_1',
                assignToVariableName: false // false if not in use
            }); 
                                                                                                                            adUnits.push({
                network: dfpNetwork,
                adunit: 'PokemonGo_Mobile_300x250_Extra_2',
                size: [[300, 250]],
                code: 'div-ad-PokemonGo_Mobile_300x250_Extra_2',
                assignToVariableName: false // false if not in use
            });  
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      
    }
    // END: Defining Adunits

    googletag.cmd.push(function() {
      if(adUnits){
        var dfpSlots = [];
        for (var i = 0, len = adUnits.length; i < len; i++) {
          dfpSlots[i] = googletag.defineSlot('/'+adUnits[i].network+'/'+adUnits[i].adunit, adUnits[i].size, adUnits[i].code).addService(googletag.pubads());
          if(adUnits[i].assignToVariableName && (adUnits[i].assignToVariableName !== null)) window[adUnits[i].assignToVariableName] = dfpSlots[i];
        }
      }
    });

    /* A9 Slots */
    if(adUnits){
        if(apstag){
          for (var i = 0, len = adUnits.length; i < len; i++) {
                  a9Slots.push({slotID: adUnits[i].code,slotName: adUnits[i].network+'/'+adUnits[i].adunit,sizes: adUnits[i].size});
              }
        }
    }
    /* A9 Request Bids */
    apstag.fetchBids({
                        slots: a9Slots,
                        timeout: TIMEOUT
                    },
                    function(bids) {
                        console.log('BDS back',(new Date()).getTime()-adsStart,bids);
                        a9BidsBack = true;
                    });

    googletag.cmd.push(function() {
        /* A9 Set Bids */
        if(a9BidsBack) apstag.setDisplayBids();
        // Header Bidding Targeting
        pbjs.que.push(function() {pbjs.setTargetingForGPTAsync();});

        if(detectWidth() >= 2200) { googletag.defineSlot('/31904509/Gamepress_Desktop_Skin_1x1', [1, 1], 'div-ad-Gamepress_Desktop_Skin_1x1').addService(googletag.pubads()); }

        // Init DFP
        googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
        googletag.pubads().collapseEmptyDivs();
        googletag.enableServices();
    });
</script>

<script type="d384d149258e51e25b630cf0-text/javascript">
  var baseURL = "https://gamepress.gg";

  function enableDM() {
    var newNode = {
      _links: {
          type: {
              href: baseURL + '/user/{user}'
          }
      },
      field_dark_mode: {
          value: 1
      }
    };
    getCsrfToken(function(csrfToken) {
        postNode(csrfToken, newNode);
    });
  }

  function getCsrfToken(callback) {
    jQuery
      .get(Drupal.url('session/token'))
      .done(function (data) {
        var csrfToken = data;
        callback(csrfToken);
      });
  }

  function patchNode(csrfToken, node) {
  var urlJSON = baseURL + '/user/' + userID2 + '?_format=hal_json'
  jQuery.ajax({
    url: urlJSON,
    method: 'PATCH',
    headers: {
      'Content-Type': 'application/hal+json',
      'X-CSRF-Token': csrfToken
    },
    data: JSON.stringify(node),
    success: function (node) {
      window.location.href = baseURL;
    }
  });
}

<script type="d384d149258e51e25b630cf0-text/javascript">

function decodeHtml(html) {
    var txt = document.createElement("textarea");
    txt.innerHTML = html;
    return txt.value;
}

function getPathByValue(value){
    for(var i = 0; i < list.length; i++){
        if(list[i].toLowerCase() == value.toLowerCase()){
            return paths[i];
        }
    }
}
/* Set the width of the side navigation to 250px */

function openNav() {
  var $slider = document.getElementById('sidenav');
  $slider.setAttribute("class", "slide-in");
  document.getElementById("overlay").style.display = "block";
  document.getElementById("menu-close").style.display = "block";
  document.getElementById("bottom-sticky-ad").style.display = "none";
  document.body.style.overflow = "hidden";
}

function closeNav() {
  var $slider = document.getElementById('sidenav');
  $slider.setAttribute("class", "slide-out");
  document.getElementById("overlay").style.display = "none";
  document.getElementById("menu-close").style.display = "none";
  document.getElementById("bottom-sticky-ad").style.display = "block";
  document.body.style.overflow = "auto";
}

</script>

<div class="field__item"><span id="topic-267591">
<div class="topic-text"> <div class="paragraph paragraph--type--text paragraph--view-mode--default">
<div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-text field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><p>This list is a comprehensive index of the overall best attackers for each and every type in Pokemon Go at the time of its current edition. If you're looking for a Pokemon to fill a niche within a specific type, then this resource is sure to lead you in the right direction.</p>
<h3>How This List is Calculated</h3>
<p>The Pokemon on this page are listed by type in descending order of power. The metric used to decide their placement is <strong>DPS^3*TDO. </strong>This metric puts a heavy emphasis on DPS, but also takes into consideration TDO in order to attempt to discover the strongest overall performance of a given Pokemon when compared to others. Because of the way that this metric works, <strong>the Pokemon here are not always ordered according to which has the highest DPS. </strong>It's entirely possible that the highest DPS option may show up 2nd or 3rd within a type if its bulk is low enough. It's also possible that Pokemon not listed on this page could potentially find niche utility in future raids, but rest assured that the Pokemon near the top of these lists are exemplary candidates for their given types.</p>
<p>If you'd like to see how these Pokemon rank yourself, we recommend that you take a look at the <strong>DPS/TDO Spreadsheet, </strong>which is what we've used to make these calculations.</p></div>
</div>
<div class="paragraph paragraph--type--featured-content paragraph--view-mode--default">
<div class="featured-1-columns-desktop featured-1-columns-mobile">
<div class="content-2-group-item ">
<a href="/pokemongo/comprehensive-dps-spreadsheet" hreflang="en"><img src="/pokemongo/sites/pokemongo/files/styles/banner_image/public/2018-08/Comprehensive-DPSTDO-Spreadsheet1.png?itok=YnSDvC-_" width="600" height="315" alt="" typeof="foaf:Image" class="image-style-banner-image" />
</a>
<a class="featured-content-title" href="/pokemongo/comprehensive-dps-spreadsheet"><span property="schema:name" class="field field--name-title field--type-string field--label-hidden">Comprehensive DPS/TDO Spreadsheet</span>
</a>
</div>
<a class="featured-button" href="/pokemongo/comprehensive-dps-spreadsheet">
Comprehensive DPS/TDO Spreadsheet
</a>
</div>
</div>
<div class="paragraph paragraph--type--text paragraph--view-mode--default">
<div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-text field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><p>In conjunction with these basic calculations, it's also worth noting that different in-game seasons bring with them temporary power boosts to specific Mega Evolved Pokemon. This is a fairly frequently changing list that will raise the placement of these Pokemon within their given types.</p></div>
</div>

        <td>
<a href="https://pokemongo.gamepress.gg/pokemon-list#psychic" target="_blank"><img src="https://pokemongo.gamepress.gg/sites/pokemongo/files/2016-07/psychic.gif" /></a>

</div>
</div>
<div class="paragraph paragraph--type--text paragraph--view-mode--default">
<div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-text field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><table>
    <tr>
        <th>Strength</th>
        <td><center><b>1</b> / 5</center></td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
        <td colspan="2">The top Bug moves are lightning fast, but it's one of the weakest types in GO.</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
        <th>Meta-relevance</th>
        <td><center><b>2</b> / 5</center></td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
        <td colspan="2">Bug isn’t highly demanded. Other stronger types usually do the job better, unless the target is doubly weak to Bug or if it's raining.</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
        <th>Future-proof</th>
        <td><center><b>1</b> / 5</center></td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
        <td colspan="2">Volcarona is the closest competitor with its solid stats. Bug also has to worry about the Ultra Beasts known as Pheromosa and Buzzwole farther down the line (Gen 7). A few of the Bug Type Mega Evolutions such as Mega Pinsir and Mega Heracross give value to our existing bugs as well.</td>
    </tr><tr>   
</tr></table></div>
</div>

</a></h2>
<a href="/pokemongo/pokemon/461" hreflang="en"><img src="/pokemongo/sites/pokemongo/files/styles/50x50/public/2018-04/461.png?itok=d05c2KKs" width="50" height="50" alt="Weavile" typeof="foaf:Image" class="image-style-_0x50" />

<div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-right-explanation field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><table><tr><th>Specialty</th>
<td>
<a href="https://pokemongo.gamepress.gg/pokemon-list#psychic" target="_blank"><img src="https://pokemongo.gamepress.gg/sites/pokemongo/files/2016-07/psychic.gif" /></a>

</td>
</tr><tr><th>Fast Move</th><td><a href="https://gamepress.gg/pokemongo/pokemon-move/snarl">Snarl</a></td></tr><tr><th>Charged Move</th><td><a href="https://gamepress.gg/pokemongo/pokemon-move/foul-play">Foul Play</a></td></tr></table></div>

</div>
<div class="paragraph paragraph--type--text paragraph--view-mode--default">
<div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-text field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><table><tr><th>Strength</th>
<td><center><b>3</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">It took a Pokemon with an Attack stat as high as Darkrai to put the top Dark attacker on parity with the top Ghost attackers. Even then, Darkrai does just as well with its Ghost type Charged Move.</td>
</tr><tr><th>Meta-relevance</th>
<td><center><b>4</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">Ghost and Dark compete for the same niche. While Ghost tends to sport higher DPS, Dark's generally superior resistances keep it competitive.</td>
</tr><tr><th>Future-proof</th>
<td><center><b>3</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">The legendary Pokemon Yveltal and Mythical Pokemon Hoopa (Gen 6) are starting to draw near. Urshifu (Gen 8) is a Mythical Pokemon with a potential signature Dark Type move, but it's a ways off. What Dark-types really have to watch out for are Ghosts, which have better moves at present.</td>
</tr><tr></tr></table></div>

<div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-right-explanation field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><table>

<div class="paragraph paragraph--type--two-column-1-4 paragraph--view-mode--default">
<div class="column-1-4-container">
<div class="field field--name-field-left-pokemon field--type-entity-reference field--label-hidden field__items">
<div class="field__item"><article id="node-293" class="" data-history-node-id="293" role="article" about="/pokemongo/pokemon/149">
<h2><a href="/pokemongo/pokemon/149" rel="bookmark"><span class="field field--name-title field--type-string field--label-hidden">Dragonite</span>
</a></h2>
<a href="/pokemongo/pokemon/149" hreflang="en"><img src="/pokemongo/sites/pokemongo/files/styles/50x50/public/2016-07/149.png?itok=NX3SBlXx" width="54" height="50" alt="Dragonite" typeof="foaf:Image" class="image-style-_0x50" />
</a>
</article></div>
</div>
<div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-right-explanation field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><table>
    <tr>
        <th>Specialty</th>
        <td>
<a href="https://pokemongo.gamepress.gg/pokemon-list#dragon" target="_blank"><img src="https://pokemongo.gamepress.gg/sites/pokemongo/files/2016-07/dragon.gif" /></a>
</td>
    </tr><tr><th>Fast Move</th><td><a href="https://gamepress.gg/pokemongo/pokemon-move/dragon-tail">Dragon Tail</a></td></tr><tr><th>Charged Move</th><td><a href="https://gamepress.gg/pokemongo/pokemon-move/outrage">Outrage</a></td></tr></table></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="paragraph paragraph--type--text paragraph--view-mode--default">
<div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-text field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><table><tr><th>Strength</th>
<td><center><b>5</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">Dragon Type is one of the few types in the game that has true "generalist" Pokemon; Pokemon so strong that they can slot into raids that they aren't super effective against and still pull their own weight. While this tactic is not recommended, the fact that it is still borderline-viable should say just how strong they are.</td>
</tr><tr><th>Meta-relevance</th>
<td><center><b>5</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">It's the top counter to myriad Dragon type legendary Pokemon of past, present, and future, and it ranks near the top of all species in neutral DPS. Keep in mind that every generation starting with 3 has had a legendary dragon thus far, and all but Dialga have been weak to Dragon.</td>
</tr><tr><th>Future-proof</th>
<td><center><b>1</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">Kyurem - Black and Kyurem - White are the closest threats. The Mega Evolved dragons are also looming on the horizon, but the fact that they can use existing Pokemon makes them less of a threat and more a bonus for what we already have. The Generation 7 Legendary Pokemon Ultra Necrozma could be a massively powerful force if it's given a Dragon Type moveset. And finally, the Generation 8 Legendary Pokemon Eternatus could be very strong given the right moveset. </td>
</tr><tr></tr></table></div>
</div>
</div></span>
</div>
<div class="field__item"> <div class="paragraph paragraph--type--scrollto paragraph--view-mode--default">
<div id="electric1"></div>
</div>

</tr><tr><th>Future-proof</th>
<td><center><b>4</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">The absolute largest threat to the Electric Type meta is the Ultra Beast Xurkitree (Gen 7). Due to its absolutely gargantuan Attack stat, it has the potential to outclass every other Electric Type, though its very wide Electric Type movepool means that its power could land basically anywhere on the board.</td>

<div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-text field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><table><tr><th>Strength</th>
<td><center><b>2</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">Fairy is generally seen as a poor man's Dragon type, though it also counters Fighting pretty hard as well.</td>
</tr><tr><th>Meta-relevance</th>
<td><center><b>3</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">See above. Fairy does have a couple of niches, which are double resisting Dragon and being boosted in the more common cloudy weather.</td>
</tr><tr><th>Future-proof</th>
<td><center><b>4</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">Fairy Types don't have much to fear. Xerneas lacks any move in its main series set that is currently a Fairy Type fast move, so the nearest threats are the Tapus from Generation 7. The Generation 8 Legendary Pokemon Zacian could topple all Fairy types in its wake thanks to its obscene Attack stat, but it currently doesn't learn any Fairy Type fast moves.</td>
</tr><tr></tr></table></div>

        <th>Specialty</th>
        <td>
<a href="https://pokemongo.gamepress.gg/pokemon-list#normal" target="_blank"><img src="https://gamepress.gg/pokemongo/sites/pokemongo/files/2016-07/normal.gif" /></a>

<a href="https://pokemongo.gamepress.gg/pokemon-list#dark" target="_blank"><img src="https://gamepress.gg/pokemongo/sites/pokemongo/files/2016-07/dark.gif" /></a>

</div>
</div>
<div class="paragraph paragraph--type--text paragraph--view-mode--default">
<div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-text field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><table>
    <tr>
        <th>Strength</th>
        <td><center><b>5</b> / 5</center></td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
        <td colspan="2">Fighting is one of the most pervasive types in the entire game, and will always have vast potential application across many important raid bosses.</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
        <th>Meta-relevance</th>
        <td><center><b>5</b> / 5</center></td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
        <td colspan="2">Fighting's huge type coverage makes it the definite answer to most common gym defenders. It's the only type that's effective vs. Normal, which is one of the most common types in the game.</td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
        <th>Future-proof</th>
        <td><center><b>4</b> / 5</center></td>
    </tr>
    <tr>
        <td colspan="2">The Fighting Type meta is fairly stable, and outside of Shadow Lucario, it probably won't shift much. Powerful Mega Evolutions such as Mega Lucario and Mega Mewtwo X are on the way, but they're more added value to our existing Pokemon. The Generation 8 Legendary Pokemon Zamazenta could pose a threat, though it currently lacks a Fighting Type Fast Move. </td>
    </tr>
   
</table></div>
</div>

<div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-text field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><table><tr><th>Strength</th>
<td><center><b>4</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">The top Fire Types all hit very hard, and tend to be competitive with other types when multiple weaknesses are viable. </td>
</tr><tr><th>Meta-relevance</th>
<td><center><b>3</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">Though Fire is effective against a respectable 4 types, those types are less represented among Tier 5 raid bosses in particular, hurting their meta relevance.</td>
</tr><tr><th>Future-proof</th>
<td><center><b>4</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">The closest threat is the Ultra Beast Blacephalon (Generation 7), which has tremendous offensive potential. Volcarona could also be good, but it won't compete for the crown.</td>
</tr></table></div>

<div class="paragraph paragraph--type--text paragraph--view-mode--default">
<div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-text field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><table><tr><th>Strength</th>
<td><center><b>4</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">The top Pokemon in this type have little to fear and can overtake the top contenders of several other types. However, the bar drops pretty quickly as you go down the list.</td>
</tr><tr><th>Meta-relevance</th>
<td><center><b>2</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">Flying has even narrower type coverage than Fire, and very few of its main targets are really represented in Tier 5 raids.</td>
</tr><tr><th>Future-proof</th>
<td><center><b>3</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">Flying is one of the most common typings in Pokemon, and as such there are many good future contenders. Up until now, few have been blessed with a competitive moveset. Right now, the biggest threat is that Rayquaza will be given its signature Flying Type move: Dragon Ascent, though the Legendary Pokemon Yveltal from Generation 6 is poised to be good as well. It will need an extremely powerful signature move to compete for the top spot, though.</td>
</tr></table></div>

<div class="paragraph paragraph--type--text paragraph--view-mode--default">
<div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-text field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><table><tr><th>Strength</th>
<td><center><b>3</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">Grass-types in GO are by no means weak, but they're frequently out-damaged by top attackers in other types without a clear weather boost.</td>
</tr><tr><th>Meta-relevance</th>
<td><center><b>4</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">Grass covers some common types and is boosted in a common weather. A fair number of raid bosses have a double weakness to Grass.</td>
</tr><tr><th>Future-proof</th>
<td><center><b>2</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">The Ultra Beast Kartana (Gen 7) is on the horizon with a monstrous Attack stat and the potential to sport an outstanding Grass Type moveset. Shaymin (Sky Forme) (Gen 4) is slated to have great offensive stats, but its moves and availability are likely to fall short of expectations.</td>
</tr></table></div>

</div>
</div>
<div class="paragraph paragraph--type--text paragraph--view-mode--default">
<div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-text field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><table><tr><th>Strength</th>
<td><center><b>3</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">Buffs to Mud-Slap and Earthquake have made Ground a more respectable attacking type, though still slightly behind the others. It usually needs a weather boost to be the clear best. </td>
</tr><tr><th>Meta-relevance</th>
<td><center><b>3</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">Ground would be an incredibly relevant type if only it were stronger, as it covers 5 types. What keeps it relevant is its niche as an Electric counter.</td>
</tr><tr><th>Future-proof</th>
<td><center><b>5</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">Aside from Primal Groudon, Mega Garchomp, and Mega Swampert, all three of which will use our existing Pokemon, Ground is a pretty stable type. The largest threat will likely come from the Generation 6 Legendary Pokemon Zygarde, and that's only if we get a new Ground Type Fast Move and one of its many signature moves turns out to be downright broken.</td>
</tr><tr></tr></table></div>
</div>

<div class="field__item"><article id="node-299051" class="" data-history-node-id="299051" role="article" about="/pokemongo/pokemon/407">
<h2><a href="/pokemongo/pokemon/407" rel="bookmark"><span class="field field--name-title field--type-string field--label-hidden">Roserade</span>
</a></h2>
<a href="/pokemongo/pokemon/407" hreflang="en"><img src="/pokemongo/sites/pokemongo/files/styles/50x50/public/2018-03/407.png?itok=auyPjrIH" width="50" height="50" alt="Roserade" typeof="foaf:Image" class="image-style-_0x50" />
</a>
</article></div>
</div>
<div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-right-explanation field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><table><tr><th>Specialty</th>
<td>
<a href="https://pokemongo.gamepress.gg/pokemon-list#grass" target="_blank"><img src="https://gamepress.gg/pokemongo/sites/pokemongo/files/2016-07/grass.gif" /></a> 
<a href="https://pokemongo.gamepress.gg/pokemon-list#fairy" target="_blank"><img src="https://gamepress.gg/pokemongo/sites/pokemongo/files/2016-07/fairy.gif" /></a>
</td>
</tr><tr><th>Fast Move</th><td><a href="https://gamepress.gg/pokemongo/pokemon-move/poison-jab">Poison Jab</a></td></tr><tr><th>Charged Move</th><td><a href="https://gamepress.gg/pokemongo/pokemon-move/sludge-bomb">Sludge Bomb</a></td></tr></table></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="paragraph paragraph--type--text paragraph--view-mode--default">
<div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-text field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><table><tr><th>Strength</th>
<td><center><b>2</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">Poison has never been a good type to attack with. It's outclassed by other types when fighting against either of the types that it's Super Effective against, and 2x weaknesses to it are exceedingly rare.</td>
</tr><tr><th>Meta-relevance</th>
<td><center><b>1</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">There is a niche for Poison countering Grass-types in cloudy weather, or countering Fairies in the absence of Metagross. For now, Poison is minimally useful in the meta.</td>
</tr><tr><th>Future-proof</th>
<td><center><b>5</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">Investment in the current top Poison Types may not be advisable, but it's fairly safe. Nihilego (Gen 7) and Naganadel (Gen 7) are the closest threats, with Eternatus (Gen 8) even farther down the line. Given the right moveset, Eternatus could actually put Poison Types on the map due to its sheer power.</td>
</tr></table></div>
</div>
</div></span>

<div class="field__item"><span id="topic-301611">
<h2 class="main-title">Psychic Type</h2>
<div class="topic-text"> <div class="paragraph paragraph--type--two-column-1-4 paragraph--view-mode--default">
<div class="column-1-4-container">
<div class="field field--name-field-left-pokemon field--type-entity-reference field--label-hidden field__items">
<div class="field__item"><article id="node-1284086" class="" data-history-node-id="1284086" role="article" about="/pokemongo/pokemon/150-shadow">
<h2><a href="/pokemongo/pokemon/150-shadow" rel="bookmark"><span class="field field--name-title field--type-string field--label-hidden">Shadow Mewtwo</span>
</a></h2>
<a href="/pokemongo/pokemon/150-shadow" hreflang="en"><img src="/pokemongo/sites/pokemongo/files/styles/50x50/public/2020-07/mew1.png?itok=aj31X_wR" width="55" height="50" alt="Shadow Mewtwo" typeof="foaf:Image" class="image-style-_0x50" />
</a>
</article></div>
</div>
<div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-right-explanation field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><table>
    <tr>
        <th>Specialty</th>
        <td>
<a href="https://pokemongo.gamepress.gg/pokemon-list#fighting" target="_blank"><img src="https://gamepress.gg/pokemongo/sites/pokemongo/files/2016-07/fighting.gif" /></a> 
<a href="https://pokemongo.gamepress.gg/pokemon-list#poison" target="_blank"><img src="https://gamepress.gg/pokemongo/sites/pokemongo/files/2016-07/poison.gif" /></a>
    </td>
    </tr><tr><th>Fast Move</th><td><a href="https://gamepress.gg/pokemongo/pokemon-move/confusion">Confusion</a></td></tr><tr><th>Charged Move</th><td><a href="https://gamepress.gg/pokemongo/pokemon-move/psystrike">Psystrike</a> </td></tr></table></div>
</div>

</a></h2>
<a href="/pokemongo/pokemon/196" hreflang="en"><img src="/pokemongo/sites/pokemongo/files/styles/50x50/public/2016-09/196.png?itok=eGKhRHoE" width="50" height="50" alt="Espeon" typeof="foaf:Image" class="image-style-_0x50" />
</a>
</article></div>
</div>
<div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-right-explanation field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><table>
    <tr>
        <th>Specialty</th>
        <td>
<a href="https://pokemongo.gamepress.gg/pokemon-list#fighting" target="_blank"><img src="https://gamepress.gg/pokemongo/sites/pokemongo/files/2016-07/fighting.gif" /></a>

    </td>
    </tr><tr><th>Fast Move</th><td><a href="https://gamepress.gg/pokemongo/pokemon-move/confusion">Confusion</a></td></tr><tr><th>Charged Move</th><td><a href="https://gamepress.gg/pokemongo/pokemon-move/psychic">Psychic</a> </td></tr></table></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="paragraph paragraph--type--text paragraph--view-mode--default">
<div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-text field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><table><tr><th>Strength</th>
<td><center><b>5</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">Let's just get this out of the way: Shadow Mewtwo is the strongest thing in the game right now. In a neutral scenario, nothing beats Shadow Mewtwo.</td>
</tr><tr><th>Meta-relevance</th>
<td><center><b>2</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">Psychic is useful in the popular Machamp raid, and that's about it. Fighting and Poison aren't well represented among raid bosses in general, both past and future.</td>
</tr><tr><th>Future-proof</th>
<td><center><b>4</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">Lunala and Solgaleo (Gen 7) are worthy competitors, though both have lower Attack. The big threat is Ultra Necrozma (Gen 7) with its high attack and plethora of signature Psychic Type moves. Mega Mewtwo Y is currently poised to take the throne of the most powerful Pokemon in the game and <i>potentially never leave</i>, but that's more a bonus for our existing Pokemon.</td>
</tr><tr></tr></table></div>
</div>

<div class="paragraph paragraph--type--text paragraph--view-mode--default">
<div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-text field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><table><tr><th>Strength</th>
<td><center><b>4.5</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">The top Rock Types tend to be fairly dominant in any raid that they join, and are featured counters against many Tier 5 raid bosses.</td>
</tr><tr><th>Meta-relevance</th>
<td><center><b>5</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">Rock Type is very relevant, and is likely to always be. Most generations have at least one legendary Pokemon weak to rock, and a huge number of general raid bosses are also weak to it as well.</td>
</tr><tr><th>Future-proof</th>
<td><center><b>5</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">As of right now, Rock is one of the safest types. Outside of moveset shake-ups or new Shadow Pokemon, the current shape of the Rock Type meta is basically set in stone for the foreseeable future.</td>
</tr><tr></tr></table></div>
</div>

<div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-text field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><table><tr><th>Strength</th>
<td><center><b>5</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">When Steel is a weakness, the top Steel Type attackers on this list are probably at the top of the counter list.</td>
</tr><tr><th>Meta-relevance</th>
<td><center><b>3</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">Steel's limited effective coverage to Fairy, Ice and Rock-types means that it doesn't get to power through raids as often as some other types.</td>
</tr><tr><th>Future-proof</th>
<td><center><b>4</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2"> The next Steel-type Pokemon who can compete is Kartana (Gen 7), an Ultra Beast. After that, Zacian (Gen 8) could be a very real contender for top Steel Type.</td>
</tr><tr></tr></table></div>

<h2><a href="/pokemongo/pokemon/130" rel="bookmark"><span class="field field--name-title field--type-string field--label-hidden">Gyarados</span>
</a></h2>
<a href="/pokemongo/pokemon/130" hreflang="en"><img src="/pokemongo/sites/pokemongo/files/styles/50x50/public/2016-07/130.png?itok=rynkp5dH" width="54" height="50" alt="Gyarados" typeof="foaf:Image" class="image-style-_0x50" />
</a>
</article></div>

<div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-right-explanation field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><table><tr><th>Specialty</th>
<td>
<a href="https://pokemongo.gamepress.gg/pokemon-list#fire" target="_blank"><img src="https://gamepress.gg/pokemongo/sites/pokemongo/files/2016-07/fire.gif" /></a>

</td>
</tr><tr><th>Fast Move</th><td><a href="https://gamepress.gg/pokemongo/pokemon-move/waterfall">Waterfall</a></td></tr><tr><th>Charged Move</th><td><a href="https://gamepress.gg/pokemongo/pokemon-move/hydro-pump">Hydro Pump</a></td></tr></table></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="paragraph paragraph--type--text paragraph--view-mode--default">
<div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-text field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><table><tr><th>Strength</th>
<td><center><b>4</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">When it shares the spotlight with other types, Water Types tend to be the dependable, all-around good options. They may not always top the DPS list, but they're usually up there somewhere.</td>
</tr><tr><th>Meta-relevance</th>
<td><center><b>4</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">Water covers some common types, making it beneficial to have a decent Water Type team ready.</td>
</tr><tr><th>Future-proof</th>
<td><center><b>4</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">The Water Type meta is pretty stable, though it will have a few Megas and Primal Kyogre appearing in the fairly near future.</td>
</tr><tr></tr></table></div>

<td>None</td>
</tr><tr><th>Fast Move</th><td><a href="https://gamepress.gg/pokemongo/pokemon-move/hidden-power">Hidden Power</a></td></tr><tr><th>Charged Move</th><td><a href="https://gamepress.gg/pokemongo/pokemon-move/giga-impact">Giga Impact</a></td></tr></table></div>

<div class="column-1-4-container">
<div class="field field--name-field-left-pokemon field--type-entity-reference field--label-hidden field__items">
<div class="field__item"><article id="node-1273626" class="" data-history-node-id="1273626" role="article" about="/pokemongo/pokemon/474-shadow">
<h2><a href="/pokemongo/pokemon/474-shadow" rel="bookmark"><span class="field field--name-title field--type-string field--label-hidden">Shadow Porygon-Z</span>
</a></h2>
<a href="/pokemongo/pokemon/474-shadow" hreflang="en"><img src="/pokemongo/sites/pokemongo/files/styles/50x50/public/2020-07/por2.png?itok=Z7uwH0Fn" width="55" height="50" alt="Shadow Porygon-Z" typeof="foaf:Image" class="image-style-_0x50" />
</a>
</article></div>
</div>
<div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-right-explanation field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><table><tr><th>Specialty</th>
<td>None</td>
</tr><tr><th>Fast Move</th><td><a href="https://gamepress.gg/pokemongo/pokemon-move/hidden-power">Hidden Power</a></td></tr><tr><th>Charged Move</th><td><a href="https://gamepress.gg/pokemongo/pokemon-move/tri-attack">Tri-Attack</a></td></tr></table></div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="paragraph paragraph--type--text paragraph--view-mode--default">
<div class="clearfix text-formatted field field--name-field-text field--type-text-long field--label-hidden field__item"><table><tr><th>Strength</th>
<td><center><b>2</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">These Pokemon could be truly great.... if their typing/movesets were anything but Normal</td>
</tr><tr><th>Meta-relevance</th>
<td><center><b>1</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">The Normal-type has generally weak candidates and zero meta relevance, being unable to hit for super effective damage.</td>
</tr><tr><th>Future-proof</th>
<td><center><b>2</b> / 5</center></td>
</tr><tr><td colspan="2">The biggest threat is probably Arceus (Gen 4)</td>
</tr><tr></tr></table></div>

<span class="remove" onclick="if (!window.__cfRLUnblockHandlers) return false; closeModalGP()" data-cf-modified-d384d149258e51e25b630cf0-=""><i class="fa fa-times-circle" aria-hidden="true"></i></span>

<script type="d384d149258e51e25b630cf0-text/javascript">
  var gpLoaded = false;
    $(document).ready(function() {
          bindButtons();
      });

    function bindButtons(){
      var showButtons = document.getElementsByClassName("show-expl");
          for(var i = 0; i < showButtons.length; i++){
            showButtons[i].onclick = showModalGP;
          }
    }

    function showModalGP(e){
      document.getElementById("site-header").style.zIndex = "0";
      var modal = document.getElementById('gp-tier-modal');
      if(!modal){
        return;
      }
      var content = $(e.target).data('content');
      var title = $(e.target).data('title');
      var titleID = title.replace(":", "");
      var explDiv = document.getElementById(titleID + "-expl-container");
      var text = decodeHtml(explDiv.innerHTML);
      title = "<div class='expl-title'>" + title + "<\/div>"
      var modal2 = document.getElementById("unit-expl-gp");
      modal2.innerHTML = title + text;
      modal.style.display = "block";
      gpLoaded = false;
    }

    function closeModalGP(){
      var modal = document.getElementById('gp-tier-modal');
      if(!modal){
        return;
      }
      modal.style.display = "none";
      gpLoaded = true;
      document.getElementById("site-header").style.zIndex = "";
    }
    $('body').click(function (e) {
        if(typeof(isDBL) == 'undefined'){
          var id = e.target.id;
        var parents = document.getElementById("modal-cont-gp-tier");
        var modal = document.getElementById("gp-tier-modal");
        if(!modal){
          return;
        }
        if(modal.style.display == "block" && gpLoaded && !(parents.contains(e.target))){
          modal.style.display = "none";
          document.getElementById("site-header").style.zIndex = "";
          gpLoaded = false;
        }
        else{
          gpLoaded = true;
        }
      }
      function decodeHtml(html) {
        var txt = document.createElement("textarea");
        txt.innerHTML = html;
        return txt.value;
    }

  });
</script>
